It addresses adults who acquired skills and competences through work but lack a formal qualification, including those who wish to access further training. The approach refers to the prevailing training regulations and occupational profiles, and leads to certificates ([128]Gleichwertigkeitsfeststellung.) expressing the extent to which the skills demonstrated are equivalent to those normally gained under the Vocational Training Act. The participating chambers of industry, commerce and trade started piloting in April 2017; interim results were presented to a broad public at a conference in Berlin in December 2017 ([129] The result of this reference project in developing a validation system will be a handbook with process description, admission criteria, instruments, certificate of validation and recommendations.<br/><br/>Assessment and recognition of foreign vocational qualifications<br/><br/>The Vocational Qualifications Recognition Act (BQFG), introduced in April 2012, provides individuals with the right to have their foreign-acquired qualifications matched to a German qualification by an appropriate authority. Depending on the sector, assessment and recognition of foreign occupational qualifications is carried out by IHK Fosa ([130] or lead chambers (Leitkammern). The implementation of the Recognition Act is monitored and documented in a yearly report ([131] In June 2017, the report evaluated the first five years of implementing the Act.<br/><br/>Information and guidance are essential to success in the recognition process. The federal government has established a range of comprehensive services, such as the Recognition in Germany website ([132] the counselling network of the Integration through qualification (IQ) programme and the Working and living in Germany telephone hotline, a project run jointly by the Federal Employment Agency and the Federal Office for Migration and Refugees ([133]Bundesamt für Migration und Flüchtlinge (BAMF).).Where documentation of the acquired qualification is missing or incomplete, a skills analysis ([134] can help to demonstrate professional competences in a practical way (via a work sample, a work test at a company or an interview). A project of the education ministry and the association of German chambers of commerce and industry, which started at the end of 2015, offers recognition consultants to provide personal consultancy for people interested in having their qualifications recognised while still in their countries of origin (ProRecognition). The funding and residency options available for upskilling training where a foreign qualification has not been judged fully equivalent to a German qualification were substantially expanded in 2015.<br/><br/>The federal government's law on assessing professional qualifications has proven an effective instrument in helping people with qualifications acquired outside Germany to integrate into the labour market and in securing a supply of skilled workers. Between 2012 and 2017, 111 500 applications for recognition were made in professions governed by federal law alone. Almost two thirds of these qualifications acquired abroad (67 500) were certified as being fully equivalent to the relevant German reference qualifications. Most of the qualifications recognised were in the regulated professions, especially in healthcare (nurse, doctor) ([135] ([136 various incentives are offered to learners, which differ for IVET and CVET learners:<br/><br/>Apprentice remuneration<br/><br/>According to the Vocational Training Act, the training company shall pay apprentices an appropriate allowance. The amount and payment procedure are specified in the training contract. Training allowances are based on collective wage agreements.<br/><br/>Average apprentice remuneration across Germany for 2017 was EUR 876 gross per month (increasing from the first year of training at EUR 794 to the fourth year at At the other end, the lowest monthly remuneration was for the apprentices as chimney sweep (EUR 518) followed by florist and baker (EUR 617 and EUR 637).<br/><br/>Financial support is offered during IVET and prevocational training organised by the federal employment agency to help apprentices overcome the economic difficulties that can stand in the way of appropriate vocational qualification. The overall monthly needs of the apprentice not living with his or her parents are estimated and the amount which cannot be covered by own/parents' income is subsidised. In 2017, 88 000 persons undergoing vocational training and 23 000 participating in pre-vocational training measures received funding and support through such a grant (from 1 August 2016 the maximum is EUR 622 per month) ([138]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn:, p. 119). There are also vocational training grants specifically adapted to the needs of learners with disabilities ([139]<br/><br/>This support is targeted at all young people who need help to start and complete vocational training. Enrolment is voluntary. Mentors help apprentices to improve German language and other academic skills through special classes during at least three hours a week. The law establishing this measure came into force in May 2015 and in 2017, 36 000 young people were beneficiaries ([141]Actual expenditures 2017: EUR 97.1 million (BMBF, 2018 p 121).). This represents a share of 2.7% of all apprentices in 2017. It helps apprentices to avoid dropping out of training, to stabilise training relationships and to complete vocational training. Six months after completing a measure, 81% of participants were in jobs subject to social insurance contributions.<br/><br/>Prevocational education and training measures as defined in the German Social Code (SGB III) prepare young people who need extra support for vocational training or, if they cannot yet start training for inherent personal reasons, to enter employment in the mainstream labour market.<br/><br/>Pre-VET measures give participants opportunities to assess their skills and abilities as part of the process of choosing a possible occupation, e.g. through internships. The measures also provide them with the knowledge and skills they need to start initial vocational training. They can support them in their preparation to acquire a secondary general school-leaving certificate or equivalent school leaving qualification; if this is not or not yet possible, it helps place participants in employment and sustainably integrate into the training and/or labour market.<br/><br/>The primary goal of introductory training is to give young people (although there is no actual age limit) with limited prospects of being placed in training an opportunity to acquire modular qualifications towards a recognised occupation. Introductory training also offers companies providing training an opportunity to get to know young people, not just in a brief job application interview, but to observe their skills and abilities over a period of six to twelve months in daily work processes.<br/><br/>Companies which offer introductory training enter into a contract with the young people concerned. Employers receive a subsidy of up to EUR 231 per month to remunerate apprentices, plus a flat-rate contribution towards the average total social security amount payable. On completion of the work placement, participants receive a certificate issued by the competent body (e.g. chamber of industry and commerce, chamber of skilled crafts). In certain circumstances, up to six months' credit for the work placement can be offset against the qualifying period of a subsequent apprenticeship. 69% of those completing introductory training transfer into training six months after completing the introductory training measure. In 2017, around 24 000 young people began introductory training ([145]Actual spending 2017: € 50 million (BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018 [Vocational education and training report 2018], Bonn: BMBF, p.118. <br/><br/>Training placements<br/><br/>Training placements are offered to all young people through employment agencies and jobcentres. The agencies also offer employers specific consultancy services and approach them to enquire about training places. In the 2016/17 reporting year, 549 785 training places and 547 824 training place applicants were registered with the federal employment agency ([146]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018.[Vocational education and training report 2018]. Bonn: BMBF, p. 118.).<br/><br/>Special measures for integrating refugees into IVET<br/><br/>Integrating young people with migration background and refugees in the education and VET system and in the labour market is a priority. Keys to integration are learning the host language, validation of formal and non-formal and informally acquired skills, provision of vocational orientation and access to pre-VET and VET programmes, apprenticeships, upskilling measures and employment. Following the arrival of about one million refugees at the end of 2015, existing programmes aiming to integrate disadvantaged groups into the labour market and the VET system opened up with an additional focus on refugees. New programmes were established in 2016, specifically addressing refugees. A synopsis of integration measures for refugees was published by the federal government in December 2016 ([147] Since 2015, a specific ESF-supported programme German for professional purposes ([148] was carried out to help people with migration background learn the German language and integrate into society and the world of work. 80 000 people participated in the programme in 2017. A new information hub for German language courses, Handbook Germany ([149] was also set up, funded by the federal office for migration and refugees (BAMF) ([150]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018, p. 57-60 and from p. 88. <br/><br/>Since a 2016 amendment to the Social Code, young refugees with tolerated residence status who participate in dual VET are entitled to financial support after 15 months' stay in Germany instead of the previously required four years. Support is in the form of training loans, pre-vocational training measures, and the so-called assisted training scheme (see above). The Integration Act ([151] and  was adopted in July 2016 and intends to facilitate refugee integration into society through a 'support and challenge' approach. Refugees with prospects of staying permanently will take integration courses at an early stage, and have legal certainty while in vocational training: up to three-year right of residence for those in apprenticeship until successful completion of training, followed by two-year right to reside, if the person works in the profession s/he was trained in. Asylum seekers will be granted temporary residence permits once they have submitted their application for asylum, so they have legal certainty and early access to the integration courses and labour market.<br/><br/>A special programme, Funding to promote the professional mobility of young people with an interest in training and unemployed young skilled workers from Europe (MobiPro-EU) develops measures and instruments to promote international mobility for apprentices in the EU. German language tuition, social and vocational training and mentoring, and financial support to enable mobility and to secure living costs help young people interested in apprenticeship and young adults from the EU to complete vocational training in a company in Germany.<br/><br/>Incentives for continuing VET learners<br/><br/>The State promotes participation in continuing VET with various support and funding instruments (grants, subsidies and loans to cover continuing VET and living costs), addressing various target groups. Some of them are regulated by law and others are in the form of programmes.<br/><br/>This law gives craftspeople and other skilled workers a statutory entitlement to financial assistance to cover costs of further training and living expenses. This financial support, jointly covered by the Federal and State governments, comprises subsidies (or, from a certain amount, bank loans at favourable rates) for a master craftsperson course and exam fees or other programmes leading to a comparable qualification. The AFBG, the equivalent to university student grants (BAföG), was amended in 2016 to improve the funding and support, and expand available funding options to new target groups. It increases VET career attractiveness.<br/><br/>In 2016, the number of funding recipients was approximately 162 000. In 2017, EUR 619 million funding was available for this programme: EUR 323 million in the form of subsidies and EUR 296 million in the form of loans. Since the Meister-BAföG was introduced in 1996, it has made it possible for around two million people to upgrade their vocational skills and achieve promotion by providing approximately EUR 8 billion in funding ([154]BMBF(2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p. 125.). AFGB is the most comprehensive continuing VET funding instrument. It is a major pillar and driver of skills upgrading and occupational advancement.<br/><br/>Since 1991, the education ministry ([156]Bundesministeriums für Bildung und Forschung (BMBF).) has offered particularly gifted young workers a specific continuing VET grant (there is a similar programme in academic education). Grants are awarded to approximately 6 000 new recipients every year and more than 133 000 grants have been provided since the programme started. Funding is provided for the measure itself, for travel and accommodation costs and for costs of work materials. Scholarship recipients may apply for a total of EUR 6 000 for an unlimited amount of continuing training courses eligible for funding within the three-year funding period. They are required to bear 10% of costs themselves per course ([157]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BIBB, p. 396. <br/><br/>The education ministry's upgrading scholarship offers incentives to study for skilled workers with professional experience, whether or not they gained a higher education entrance qualification at school. It was established for professionals with at least two years' work experience and with outstanding talents. When qualified skilled professionals are already working, financial issues often prevent them from starting a course of studies. It is the only academic programme supporting talented students who are combining work and study (over a third of the scholarship holders) or studying full-time for the duration of their course of studies (standard prescribed study period). The funding provided for full-time study is EUR 815 a month (plus a one-off childcare payment) and EUR 2 400 a year offered for those combining work and study ([159]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BIBB, p. 399.  Scholarships are awarded to approximately 1 000 new recipients every year and about 9 900 were provided from 2008 to 2017 ([160]Funding volume in 2017: EUR 24.8 million.).<br/><br/>To encourage groups of people that tend to have lower rates of participation in company-based continuing vocational training (workers on low incomes, women, employees in small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs), people working part-time and healthcare professionals), the federal government approved an additional financing scheme in 2008: premium and savings vouchers. The premium voucher reduces training costs by up to 50% of tuition fees (max EUR 500) for job-related training courses or courses that help improve people's employability. It targets employees and the self-employed who work at least 15 hours a week and have a maximum taxable annual income of EUR 20 000 (or 40 000 for couples; child allowances are taken into account) or are on parental leave. The voucher is valid for six months. People can receive vouchers every two years. This measure is supported by the European Social Fund. The savings voucher provides a right to withdraw money from capital formation saving plans without losing the savings grant. This is open to all people who have such saving plans, regardless of their income. Since the programme started in 2008, around 320 000 premium vouchers have been issued and 28 000 individual continuing VET savings plans established.<br/><br/>Continuing VET for the unemployed<br/><br/>One important national strategy is the prevention of unemployment through nation-wide standard (under the German Social Code, SGB III) upskilling programmes, specifically addressing those at risk of long-term unemployment: the low-skilled and the unemployed ([162]Huismann, A. (2018). Guidance and outreach for inactive and unemployed – Germany. Cedefop ReferNet thematic perspectives series. The federal government implements active labour market policy (ALMP) measures addressing long-term unemployment.<br/><br/>To be eligible for a continuing VET voucher, participation must be considered necessary to enable occupational integration, to avert pending unemployment or because the candidate does not have a vocational qualification. When identifying the need for continuing VET measures, the employment agency or the authority providing basic income support for jobseekers must always consider labour market conditions. They must decide, among others, whether the candidate could find employment without continuing VET; whether other labour market policy instruments could be more appropriate; and whether the candidate could, in all likelihood, return to the labour market as a result of the training.<br/><br/>Persons meeting the general eligibility criteria are granted an education and training voucher (Bildungsgutschein) by the employment agency or the authority providing jobseeker support. This voucher contains data on the education objective, the time required to reach this objective and information as to where the voucher applies in the region. The holder can redeem it at any education institution of their choice which is accredited for funding under the conditions specified in the education voucher. The continuing VET activity must also be approved for funding and support. The education institution then charges the employment agency for the course costs on the basis of the education voucher. Information on approved continuing VET measures and providers can also be found in the database of the federal employment agency ([163]KURSNET: <br/><br/>By issuing an education and training voucher, the reimbursement of some or all of the following continuing VET expenses is confirmed: course costs, travel expenses, costs for external board and lodging, and childcare expenses. Candidates are also entitled to receive unemployment benefit for the duration of the continuing VET programme if specific requirements are met. Regulations related to unemployment benefits remain unchanged for the duration of the continuing VET programme.<br/><br/>The 2016 law to reinforce continuing VET and unemployment insurance coverage (AWStG)<br/><br/>Workers with low-level qualifications, the long-term unemployed and older employees in particular must be increasingly recruited into vocational further training. Qualifying further vocational training should also strengthen participants' motivation, resilience and basic skills and reduce the rate at which people drop out of continuing training. To achieve these goals, the Federal Ministry of Labour and Social Affairs (BMAS) expanded support and funding for further vocational training through a law to strengthen continuing VET and unemployment insurance coverage (AWStG) ([164] this came into force in 2016. The law improves access and the overall conditions of continuing VET (such as allowances during training and financial incentives for passing exams) in order to attract more people with few or low-level qualifications, the long-term unemployed and older employees into qualifying continuing vocational training. This new law complements and reinforces standard continuing VET support instruments under the German Social Code, as in the following examples.<br/><br/>This is available both to the unemployed and employees under threat of imminent unemployment, as well as to workers with low levels of qualifications and employees in SMEs. Eligibility for funding also depends on labour market conditions, as with the education and training voucher. Eligible continuing VET courses aiming to obtain, update or upgrade a vocational (also partial) qualification are listed in the KURSNET ([166] database of the federal employment agency.<br/><br/>Based on the German Social Code, this gives people with low-level qualifications living in structurally weak areas the opportunity to acquire a recognised vocational qualification or complete modular (partial) qualifications. Target groups are the unemployed and people at risk of becoming unemployed. Since 2012 the initiative is also helping those returning to work who have no VET qualifications (or have not worked in the occupation they trained for over four years) to get back into jobs subject to social insurance contributions.<br/><br/>Employment agencies can provide full or partial funding for qualification courses for employees aged over 45 working in SMEs with fewer than 250 employees. Since April 2012, such employees can also receive funding for continuing VET, regardless of their current qualification level, on the additional provision that their employer meets at least 50% of the course costs. Employees who have no or no useful vocational qualifications can also receive funding. Employers who release employees with low-level qualifications to take part in continuing VET to gain qualifications can receive a subsidy to cover the employee's pay for the period they spend in training. The changed prerequisites for funding resulted in a significant increase in participation rates. WeGebAU has also been increasingly used to help employed geriatric nursing assistants upgrade their qualifications ([169]This section is based on: Hippach-Schneider, U.; Huismann, A. (2019). Vocational education and training in Europe: Germany. Cedefop ReferNet VET in Europe reports 2018.<br/><br/>For many German companies, it is a tradition and a matter of course to provide and to carry most of the costs for apprenticeship. However, the readiness to provide apprenticeship has been declining in the last decade (in 2007, 24.1% of companies against 19.8% in 2016), especially among the smallest companies (1 to 9 employees) who face increasing difficulties in filling the apprenticeship places they offer. This shows that companies, especially small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs), need support, which is provided in various forms, as described below ([170]For further information on this, please consult: Hippach-Schneider, U.; Huismann, A. (2019). Vocational education and training in Europe: Germany. Cedefop ReferNet VET in Europe reports 2018. <br/><br/>Inter-company vocational training centres and training structures<br/><br/>SMEs, in particular crafts companies, are important training suppliers, but are unable, or not fully able, to provide all the facets of training required by regulations. This is primarily due to the increasing division of labour in production processes, increasing specialisation and, in some cases, financial problems or accelerated technological change. The limited suitability of such enterprises as training providers is compensated for by supplementary external training measures in inter-company vocational training centres or through training structures. Inter-company training centres also have an essential position in further and continuing training in SMEs, especially in the commercial and technical sectors. Such training centres also exist in the skilled trade sector ([171] Funding is offered for the modernising and restructuring of inter-company training centres to adapt them to changing education and training policy and economic conditions, as well as the challenge of digitalisation.<br/><br/>As of 2016, a process to help find training places / apprentices has been put in place: every young person who is still looking for an apprenticeship on 30 September of a given year will receive three offers of company-based training from an employment agency.<br/><br/>Jobstarter plus<br/><br/>The federal ministry of education funds and supports projects in the national JOBSTARTER plus programme ([173]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p. 93.) with part-finances from the European Social Fund (ESF) to improve regional training structures and trial innovative training policy approaches to solving training market problems. The programme is designed to respond flexibly and actively to current training market developments with a range of variable funding priorities:<br/><br/>advise and support SMEs in the process of (re-) starting participation in dual training and increasing their commitment to training;<br/><br/>counteract matching problems and the difficulties that companies have in filling training places in certain industries;<br/><br/>advising and supporting SMEs in the process of adapting their training to the challenges posed by the increasing automation and digitalisation of the economy.<br/><br/>The Passgenaue Besetzung programme ([175]BMBF(2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p. 122.), financed jointly by the ESF and federal ministry for economic affairs ([176]Bundesministerium für Wirtschaft und Energie, BMWi.), works to counteract matching problems in the training market. The programme provides funding for consultants who support SMEs in filling the training places they offer with suitable local and foreign young people and young refugees and migrants. Since the programme began in 2007, Passgenaue Besetzung has successfully placed around 80 000 young people in training and 9 500 in introductory training.<br/><br/>The federal employment agency (BA) supports personnel development measures in SMEs as part of its preventative approach to securing a supply of skilled workers. It informs and advises employers and identifies the possibilities for further developing the potential in companies through company-based qualification measures. This consultancy makes employers aware of the advantages of more frequently including groups of employees who are often not considered for participation in measures (e.g. those without formal qualifications and older employees) in further training measures. By offering consultancy on qualification and support for personnel development to employers, the federal employment agency is helping companies to fill training and employment vacancies from within their own ranks ([178]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p. 124.).<br/><br/>Support measures to help integrate refugees in dual VET and work<br/><br/>The following support measures, helping to integrate refugees in apprenticeship, address especially SMEs and skilled trade companies:<br/><br/>the network Companies integrate refugees funded by the federal ministry for economic affairs ([179]Bundesministerium für Wirtschaft und Energie (BMWi).) and the umbrella organisation of the chambers of industry and commerce (DIHK) is aimed at companies that are involved, or want to get involved, with refugees. The aim is to bring refugees to training and employment. The network offers its more than 1 650 member companies (three quarters of which are SMEs) the opportunity to exchange experiences and practical information on the employment of refugees;<br/><br/>the chambers' Welcome guides (Willkommenslotsen) are available to companies on all issues relating to the operational integration of refugees. Since the start of the programme in March 2016, the Welcome guides have achieved around 11 500 placements of refugees in employment, training or internship ([180]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p.94.);<br/><br/>by means of a matching process, the online internship platform JOIN ([181] offers opportunities for companies and refugees to find and get to know each other through internship placements. The aim is to speed up integration into the labour market and to remove obstacles to employment. This joint initiative of the federal ministry of the interior and business looks to offer refugees the possibility of employment in a timely manner and to provide a first proof of their qualifications, even before they receive a residence permit and a work permit ([182]This section is based on: Hippach-Schneider, U.; Huismann, A. (2019). Vocational education and training in Europe: Germany. Cedefop ReferNet VET in Europe reports 2018. <br/><br/>Guidance and counselling provision is embedded in Germany's overall employment strategy as well as in its education sector and lifelong learning strategy. Labour market policy has a long tradition of guidance and counselling; however, lifelong learning and lifelong and life-wide guidance and counselling have only recently become high-level topics on the political agenda. Due to the country's constitution and its federal structure with split responsibilities between the Federal Government, sixteen State governments and local municipalities, and between education, labour and youth ministries, guidance policy and provision is also split between these sectors. Although there are several institutional links and cooperation agreements between labour market and education policy, there is so far no coherent cross-sectoral national lifelong guidance strategy.<br/><br/>Since the 1920s, vocational guidance and counselling for youth and adults has been a legal obligation of the federal employment agency (BA) and its local employment agencies. Until 1998, the BA had a State monopoly on vocational guidance and counselling for young people moving from school to work. The BA also offers guidance and counselling services for adults, although there are multiple providers in this area, including further training institutions, some municipalities, non-profit organisations and private career counselling practitioners. Since the abolishment of the State monopoly, the private and semi-private market has grown considerably. This is partly due to limited regulations, such as concerning finances and providers' facilities (SGB III, § 289), with no stipulated qualification requirements for staff or quality standards. Nevertheless, the BA is still the largest and most important guidance and counselling service provider. This includes services for long-term unemployed from jobcentres under the social code (SGB II) ([183]Huismann, A. (2018). Guidance and outreach for inactive and unemployed – Germany. Cedefop ReferNet thematic perspectives series, pp. 13-16. <br/><br/>Guidance and counselling in the education sector mainly focuses on vocational education, advice on educational career paths or individual learning difficulties. Services vary between States and schools. Following a formal agreement between the standing conference of ministers for education and cultural affairs of the States (KMK) and the BA, school career education and the local employment agencies' vocational guidance services cooperate closely (KMK/BA 2004/17) ([184]<br/><br/>(a) vocational education is an established element in general education curricula. It is embedded in different school subjects such as work-studies (Arbeitslehre), economics and social studies, home economics, engineering, and polytechnic education. Vocational education in class is normally supported by a career counsellor from the local employment agency and supplemented in years 8, 9 or 10 by visits to the vocational information centre, to enterprises and by compulsory one- to three-week work placements in enterprises;<br/><br/>(c) practice-oriented, systematic vocational guidance is being provided at inter-company vocational training centres and similar vocational training facilities as part of a specific career guidance programme (Berufsorientierungsprogramm, BOP) to make the transition from (compulsory) general education to apprenticeships (dual vocational training) easier for learners. The BMBF supports these centres financially to help them fulfil this task. The programme started in 2008 and was established permanently in 2010. These measures give young people the opportunity to spend two weeks at a vocational training facility gaining practical experience in three occupation-specific areas related to their potential. The aim is to achieve a sustainable improvement in school-to-work transition management ([187]<br/><br/>Vocational guidance, work studies and initiatives to ease transition from school to apprenticeships/work have received more attention due to the risk of dropouts, low performers and unemployment. Programmes like the Educational chains initiative (Bildungsketten) (see below) and Career start mentors (Berufseinstiegsbegleiter) ([188] provide individual coaching and support for learners at risk. Regional transition management (Regionales Übergangsmanagement) ([189] focuses on placing less able school leavers into apprenticeships to match demand from enterprises and provide suitable training opportunities for all school leavers.<br/><br/>This initiative aims to secure young people's success in education and training and to develop a structured and consistent funding and support policy of the Federal government (BMBF, BMAS), the federal employment agency (BA) and federal States for a vocational orientation and transition system. It focuses on analysing the potential of young people at an early stage (from grade 7), action-oriented career orientation options such as the vocational guidance programme Discover your talent (BOP), vocational orientation measures as defined in the German Social Code (SGB), individual career start coaching, mentoring through training by volunteers, introductory training, support for apprentices during training and assisted training. To extend the range of the Educational chains initiative, the BMBF started facilitating agreements between the BA and Federal and State governments in 2014. This close and binding cooperation clarifies funding structures for vocational guidance and the transition from school into work ([193]BMBF (2018). Berufsbildungsbericht 2018. Bonn: BMBF, p. 90. <br/><br/>The website  provides information and supports young people with their career choice, with a brief to disregard gender clichés.<br/><br/>In addition to regular student counselling services, universities have increasingly established career services to ease the transition from academic education to the labour market. In 2014 the BMBF started an initiative to attract university dropouts (dropout rate of 29% in bachelor courses) into vocational training ([194]<br/><br/>Some large municipalities began to establish education guidance services in the 1980s to ensure independent and high quality service delivery for citizens aiming to take up further education (Kommunale Bildungsberatung). Due to financial constraints, many of them had to close down, and by the end of the 20th century there was a lack of independent guidance provision, especially for adults and employed persons. In order to implement and support the lifelong learning strategy, the BMBF launched a Learning regions network in 2001. With ministerial funding, local and regional networks were established to initiate regional lifelong learning and employment strategies, including guidance and counselling provision. Training providers, employment agencies, chambers of commerce, enterprises, local schools and municipalities, trade unions, as well as other local actors and stakeholders participated in these networks. In most cases, guidance services formed an integral part.<br/><br/>The follow-up programme, Local learning (Lernen vor Ort), was designed to support municipalities in their efforts to establish efficient education management systems. This included educational monitoring and guidance. The programme helped establish or maintain many municipal career guidance services.'Transferinitiative Kommunales Bildungsmanagement ([195] is a structural funding programme that builds on the results of the BMBF's Local learning funding programme. The programme's fundamental idea is to optimise local government coordination of education and training.<br/><br/>In addition to these comprehensive guidance services, there are numerous specific services addressing, for example, women entering or re-entering the labour market, people with disabilities, people with migrant backgrounds ([196] and disadvantaged youths and refugees. Some services are provided by non-profit organisations, funded either by federal or State ministries or by public employment services. Some of them work only on a temporary financial basis and are not always well connected to other mainstream guidance services.<br/><br/>Data about these programmes are not fully recorded in the ISCED-97 statistics for two reasons. The majority of participants do not have a secondary school leaving certificate. However, this can be acquired in the course of the BVJ, thus improving the holder's prospects in the market for training positions;<br/><br/>basic vocational training year (Berufsgrundbildungsjahr – BGJ): basic vocational education can be completed either as a year at school (full-time) or in joint fashion at an enterprise and school. Successful completion of the BGJ can be credited as the first year of vocational training in the training occupations assigned to the relevant occupational field. In the BGJ, learners receive basic educational knowledge in a specific occupational field (e.g., metalworking techniques, electrical engineering, business and administration);<br/><br/>Introductory training (Einstiegsqualifizierung – EQ): EQ provides young people whose prospects of being placed in VET are limited due to individual reasons with an opportunity to acquire or enhance personal and vocational competences and gives companies offering training the chance to get to know these young people. It has proved to be a 'door-opener" to apprenticeship for approx. 70% of participants.<br/><br/>Young people and adults with social disadvantages, learning difficulties or handicap or insufficient German language skills (migrants) have different possibilities for pre-vocational education and training measures.<br/><br/>Entry requirements for learners (qualification/education level, age)<br/><br/>The minimum entry requirement is the lower secondary school leaving certificate for BGJ and EQ; for the BVJ, the certified attendance of grade 1 to 9 is enough.<br/><br/>Assessment of learning outcomes<br/><br/>Information not available<br/><br/>Diplomas/certificates provided<br/><br/>a) BVJ: lower secondary school certificate, in case not yet obtained;<br/><br/>b) Successful completion of the BGJ can be credited as the first year of vocational training in the training occupations assigned to the relevant occupational field;<br/><br/>c) EQ does not lead to a certificate but it has proved to be a 'door-opener" to apprenticeship for approx. 70% of participants.<br/><br/>Examples of qualifications<br/><br/>In the BGJ, learners receive basic educational knowledge in a specific occupational field (e.g., metalworking techniques, electrical engineering, business and administration).<br/><br/>Progression opportunities for learners after graduation<br/><br/>Progression is possible to school-based VET programmes and apprenticeship programmes (even in the 2nd year, in case of the BGJ).<br/><br/>Share of learners in this programme type compared with the total number of VET learners<br/><br/>Information not available<br/><br/>The share of apprentices having taken part in such a so-called transition or preparatory VET programme before starting the apprenticeship amount to approx. 9% (2016: 45 585 out of 509 997 first-year-apprentices) ([203]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018, p. 142.  ).<br/><br/>Apprenticeship scheme (dual system: duale Ausbildung) according to the Vocational Training Act (BBiG) and the Crafts Code (HwO) at EQF level 3-4 and ISCED level 354 (in 2017: 327 programmes, one for each occupation that can be learnt in the apprenticeship scheme).<br/><br/>According to the Vocational Training Act (BBiG), the training company shall pay apprentices an appropriate allowance. The amount and payment procedure are specified in the training contract. The training allowances are based on collective wage agreements and increase with every year of training, averaging about a third of the starting pay for a trained skilled worker.<br/><br/>Average apprentice remuneration across Germany for 2017 was EUR 876 gross per month (increasing from 1st year of training: EUR 794 to 4th year: On the other end, the lowest monthly remuneration was for the apprentices as chimney sweeper (EUR 518) followed by florist and baker (EUR 617 and EUR 637).<br/><br/>Is it available for adults?<br/><br/>Y<br/><br/>ECVET or other credits<br/><br/>Information not available<br/><br/>Learning forms (e.g. dual, part-time, distance)<br/><br/>school-based and practical learning in schools and inter-company vocational training centres (überbetriebliche Berufsbildungsstätten, ÜBS), (e.g. one or two days per week or one week per month);<br/><br/>company-based learning (share of approx. 70%).<br/><br/>The system is described as dual because training is conducted in two places of learning: companies and vocational schools. Apprentices attend a vocational school one or two days per week, where they are mainly taught theoretical and practical knowledge related to their occupation; they attend classes on general subjects such as economics, social studies and foreign languages. Systematic teaching at vocational school is a necessary supplement to process-oriented training within a company, which is more based on specific in-company requirements. The primary aim of training is to enable young people to acquire comprehensive vocational competence. Training programmes are designed on the principle that they should be as broad as possible and as specific as necessary.<br/><br/>Main providers<br/><br/>Companies in cooperation with vocational schools<br/><br/>Apprenticeship places are offered in both enterprises and public institutions. The professional competences to be acquired through in-company training are specified in training regulations and included by the training enterprise in an individual training plan. The binding requirements of the training regulations guarantee a uniform national standard. The BIBB is responsible for promoting inter-company training centres and supporting the planning, establishment and development of these facilities. Since 2016, an additional programme is promoting the digital transformation of these training centres by funding the purchase of digital equipment as well as selected pilot projects on adaptation of teaching and learning processes ([205 large enterpriseCompletion of full-time compulsory education, no further requirements for access (but companies select their apprentices).<br/><br/>The majority of apprentices206]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018, p. 132.  ). This group followed successivelyboth paths of education at upper secondary level: first the general, followed by the vocational qualification. Indeed, despite being classified as 'upper secondary', initial VET is also considered by high-school graduates as an alternative option to tertiary education.<br/><br/>Assessment of learning outcomes<br/><br/>A final exam is testing the practical and general knowledge of the learner based on the work requirements and processes of the occupation. As a rule, a final exam covers four or five fields relevant to the occupation. Performance in general subjects is evaluated via school reports. The exams are regulated by law (Vocational Training Act – BBiG) and is performed by the chambers. For this task, the chambers are authorised by the state and are officially acting as a public institution. Upon passing the final examination, apprentices receive a chamber certificate to document that training has been successfully completed. This certification of qualification is fully recognised and highly trusted among employers.<br/><br/>In 2016, 431 667 apprentices took the final exams ([207]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018, p. 162.  ). The success rate was 92.6%, and after retaking the exam by those who first missed, even 99.4% in total. The repartition of exam participants according to the economic sector of occupation was as follows: 63.3% in trade and industry, 23% in craft sector, 8% in liberal professions, 2.7% in public sector, 2.6% in agriculture and 0.4% in housekeeping.<br/><br/>In general, graduates of dual apprenticeship programmes are fully qualified to enter the labour market and most of them do so.<br/><br/>Those who successfully completed their apprenticeship programme, have several possibilities to further progress to post-secondary programmes, such as specialised and technician programmes, or and master craftsperson. Access to certain tertiary vocational programmes are restricted to related subject of the graduate's apprenticeship programme. Short term apprenticeship programmes do not always provide access to tertiary education programmes.<br/><br/>Destination of graduates<br/><br/>Graduates of dual apprenticeship programmes are fully qualified to enter the labour market and most of them do so. They have very good prospects of finding a work placement in a short delay.<br/><br/>Awards through validation of prior learning<br/><br/>Y<br/><br/>The most important tool for assessing non-formal learning outcomes is admission to final examinations under Section 45 (2) of the Vocational Training Act (BBiG), known as the 'Externen-Prüfung' (examination for external candidates, i.e., those not involved in a formal vocational training programme). Under this provision, people can be admitted to a final examination for a recognised occupation requiring formal training (training occupation) if they furnish evidence that they have been employed in the relevant occupation for a period at least one and a half times as long as prescribed for the period of initial training.<br/><br/>General education subjects<br/><br/>Y<br/><br/>General subjects such as mathematics, economics, social studies and foreign languages, depending on the programme<br/><br/>Key competences<br/><br/>Y<br/><br/>The primary aim of apprenticeship is to enable young people to acquire comprehensive vocational competence. Apprenticeship programmes are designed on the principle that they should be as broad as possible and as specific as necessary. After finishing the apprenticeship, they should be able to fulfil their duties as employees efficiently, effectively, innovatively, autonomously and in cooperation with others.<br/><br/>The professional competences to be acquired through in-company training are specified in training regulations and included by the training enterprise in an individual training plan. The binding requirements of the training regulations guarantee a uniform national standard.<br/><br/>For teaching in vocational schools, a framework curriculum is drawn up for every recognised training occupation in accordance with the training regulations.<br/><br/>Application of learning outcomes approach<br/><br/>As part of the implementation of the DQR (German qualification framework), the Federal Institute for Vocational Education and Training (BIBB), together with the social partners and the ministries, adopted in June 2014 a recommendation of the BIBB Board on the structure and design of training regulations which addresses the issue of competence orientation.<br/><br/>According to this recommendation, the Vocational Training Act equates vocational action capacity with the DQR's understanding of action competence. The four competence dimensions of the DQR are to be systematically taken into account in all training regulations that are to be developed from 2015 onwards, so that competence orientation is increasingly incorporated into the regulatory work."<br/><br/>Share of learners in this programme type compared with the total number of VET learners<br/><br/>The data available is on a different base: More than two thirds (68.5%) of new entrants in upper secondary VET programmes in 2017 chose the dual apprenticeship scheme (dual system), while 31.5% enrolled in a school-based VET programme. ([211]BIBB (2018). Datenreport zum Berufsbildungsbericht 2018, p. 86 (iABE).  ) secondary places Qualifications at the labour ministry coordinates the development of national policies and strategies for training for unemployed and employees, leading to the acquisition of training of teachers (10 hours) is designed so as to include obligatory practical training, which is carried out through doing teacher observation (60 hours), ongoing teaching<br/><br/> the imprisoned outcomes | tá cáilíochtaí ardleibhéil (57.9% in 2017 i gcomparáid le meán AE 46.1%), de bharr an dara céim den CTET, ar daoine iad a fhaightear go príomha;<br/><br/>an scéim phrintíseachta (déchóras) ag an leibhéal meán-mheánúil uachtarach (EQF 4) is mó an colún den VET agus cumasaíonn sí aistriú éifeachtúil ó thaobh na scoile go hobair agus dífhostaíocht i measc an aosa óig íseal;<br/><br/>dlúthchomhar idir fostóirí, ceardchumainn agus an rialtas maidir le GG a mhúnlú agus a chur chun feidhme;<br/><br/>Is príomhfhachtóir é ardoiliúint ghairmiúil ag leibhéal na treasach (EQF 6-7), rud a fhágann go bhfuil cáilíocht mar mháistircheardaí, teicneoir agus speisialtóireachta, a chuireann le tarraingteacht chonair VET.<br/><br/>Feictear gur múnla rathúil í VET na Gearmáine, bunaithe ar an gcóras déach (printíseach) den chuid is mó, rud a fhágann go bhfuil cáilíochtaí ghairmeacha ar ardchaighdeán ann. Cuireann printíseachtaí ar chumas an oideachais réidh aistriú a dhéanamh ar obair, rud a fhágann go bhfuil dífhostaíocht íseal i measc an aosa óig (2015: 7.2% de na 15 go 24 bliana d’aois) i gcomparáid le 20.4% san AE-28).<br/><br/>Roghnaíonn thart ar dhuine in dhá chéim thánaisteacha clár gairmoideachas; bíonn 70% de na daoine páirteach i bpríntíseach. Tá cáilíocht iontrála ardoideachais ag sciar méadaitheach an méid sin, ar clár é ina léirítear tarraingteacht na printíseachta. Cuireann cláir staidéir dé-chéime ag leibhéal na treaslainne agus ardoiliúna ar chumas cáilíochtaí meán agus barrbhainistíochta a fháil i gcuideachtaí.<br/><br/>Cinntíonn caighdeáin náisiúnta agus rialacháin oiliúna (churaclaim do chomhpháirteanna laistigh den chuideachta agus scoil-bhunaithe) rath na gclár dé-oiliúna. Cuireann cuideachtaí oiliúint ar fáil i gcomhréir leis na rialacháin ghairmoiliúna, arna bhforbairt ag na ceithre chomhpháirtí (rialtais cónaidhme agus Stáit, cuideachtaí agus ceardchumainn). Leis na rialacháin seo, ceadaítear solúbthacht a thabhairt do na comhlachtaí atá ag plé le printísigh. Tá an fhoghlaim ag an ngairmscoil bunaithe ar chreat-chúrsa dírithe ar rialacháin oiliúna, arna dtarraingt suas do gach slí bheatha aitheanta oiliúna.<br/><br/>Ráthaíonn athbhreithnithe rialta ar rialacháin oiliúna luas a choinneáil le hathruithe tapa teicneolaíochta agus eagraíochtúla. Tagann an tionscnamh chun próifíl saothair iomlán nua a nuashonrú nó a fhorbairt ó chomhpháirtithe sóisialta nó ón Institiúid Chónaidhme VET[2]. Tar éis dul i gcomhairle leis na páirtithe go léir atá i gceist, cinneann an t-ordlathas inniúil ar cheart dul ar aghaidh. Gné lárnach de VET is ea comhar idir stát agus comhpháirtithe sóisialta: is é sin an bealach chun a áirithiú go nglacfar le hathchóirithe VET.<br/><br/>Is cur chuige eile é an córas GG do na Gearmáine i dtaobh conas inniúlachtaí gairme a fháil, coincheap na ‘inniúlacht ghairme mar a thugtar air’: an cur chuige iomlánaíoch agus comhtháite seo i leith na hinniúlachtaí le linn conarthaí VET a fháil bunaithe ar chur chuige na dtorthaí foghlama i leith chreat um cháilíochtaí Eorpacha (EQF).<br/><br/>Tháinig méadú ar líon na n-áiteanna oiliúna nach bhfuil líonta le déanaí arís, rud a léiríonn gur gá réiteach a fháil ar sholáthar agus éileamh agus difríochtaí suntasacha réigiúnacha agus brainse á gcur san áireamh. Cuirtear cúnamh aonair ar fáil d’iarratasóirí nár éirigh leo agus treoir d’fhiontair bheaga agus mheánmhéide i gcás fadhbanna le meaitseáil. Tá gealltanas tugtha ag an gComhaontas um Oiliúint Tosaigh agus Breisoideachas gach iarratasóir i VET a chomhtháthú, lena n-áirítear iad siúd ó phoist thosaigh neamhfhabhracha, trí bhearta réamh-GG, trí chúnamh agus tacaíocht le linn na hoiliúna. Chun cosc a chur ar dhaoine titim amach oiliúna, cuireann saineolaithe sinsearacha oiliúint ar fáil do phrintíseachtaí.<br/><br/>Nua-aoisiú agus forbairt a dhéanamh ar phróifílí gairme nua d'fhonn digitiú a dhéanamh orthu<br/><br/>Tá tionchar ag an nuálaíocht dhigiteach ar phróifílí cáilíochta agus ar churaclam.Aithníonn an tionscnamh VET 4.0 éilimh i gcáilíocht oibrithe oilte agus conas freagairt do dhúshlán na digiteála.<br/><br/>Ag méadú tarraingteacht VET<br/><br/>Tá feachtas mór meán-mheánaoiseach faisnéise maidir le printíseachtaí curtha i bhfeidhm go forleathan anois ó gach scoil, i meánscoileanna ginearálta. Tá tairseacha VET ar líne ag tabhairt aghaidh ar spriocghrúpaí sonracha cosúil le mná óga nó titim amach ollscoile.<br/><br/>imircigh agus dídeanaithe a lánpháirtiú san oideachas agus san oiliúint Daonra in 2018: 82 1972 351 ([4]NB: Sonraí don daonra amhail an 1 Eanáir.<br/><br/>Tháinig méadú 2.8% air ón mbliain 2013 i leith mar gheall ar an imirce (glan-imirce in 2015: +1.1 milliún) 32 sa bhliain 2015 go 55 bliana d’aois, beidh athruithe suntasacha sa struchtúr aoise mar thoradh ar an gcion de bharr na cion ard daonra meán-aois atá ann faoi láthair, nuair a théann siad isteach sa ghrúpa 65+ bliain d’aois. In 2015, bhí 13.2% den daonra faoi bhun 14, 65.8% idir 15 agus 65, agus 21% bhí sé 65 nó níos sine. Faoin mbliain 20, beidh 13.8% den daonra faoi bhun 14, ach ní bheidh ach 55.6% idir 15-64 bliain d’aois, i.e. aois oibre. Méadóidh líon 65+ duine atá 65 bliana d’aois go 30.6 %.<br/><br/>Tá níos lú daoine óga le himeacht ama ann agus iad ag roghnú ardoideachais. Míníonn sé seo i bpáirt an líon ard áiteanna printíseachta gan líonadh. Eacnamaíocht:<br/><br/>Ba iad an chuid is mó de na cuideachtaí in 2016 (3.46 milliún fiontar, 99.6%) cuideachtaí micrea (1-9 fostaithe) agus fiontair bheaga agus mheánmhéide, (FBManna, 10-249 fostaí): bhí thart ar 3.1 milliún (thart ar 90% de na cuideachtaí go léir) ina micreafhiontair. Ní raibh níos mó ná 249 fostaí ag ach 14 630 fiontar. San iomlán, d’oibrigh 61% de na 29.1 milliún fostaí i micrea agus, FBManna: micrifhiontair atá fostaithe faoi 19% de dhaoine gníomhacha, fiontair bheaga (10-49 fostaí), thart ar 23.2%, agus fiontair mheánmhéide (50-249 fostaí), timpeall 19.3%. Is iad na cuideachtaí micrea-chuideachta agus FBManna seo atá mar lárionad Mittelst, atá ag cur ról mór sa chóras dé-VET ar na socrúcháin is phrintíseachtaí (1.12 milliún printíseacht i 2016 in aghaidh 450 000 i gcuideachtaí mhóra a bhfuil níos mó ná 249 fostaí acu) ([7]BBB (20) Dátareport zum Berfbidungsbericht 2018[Sonraí tuarascáil ar an ngairmoideachas agus ar an ngairmoiliúint 2018.] Bonn: BBB. p.206 freisin: Féach:<br/><br/>In 2017, bhí an chuid is mó de dhaoine fostaithe (74.5%) ag obair san earnáil eacnamaíoch threasach (seirbhísí den chuid is mó), agus 24.1% ag obair san earnáil thánaisteach (tionscal táirgeachta) agus 1.4% ag obair san earnáil phríomhoideachais (talmhaíocht, foraoise agus iascaireacht) ([8] Torthaí na gcuntas fostaíochta laistigh de na cuntais náisiúnta (VR).<br/><br/>Le blianta beaga anuas, tá laghdú tagtha ar sciar na bhfiontar san earnáil phríomhthréimhseach a sholáthraíonn socrúcháin phrintísigh agus tá an líon sin ag dul i laghad in 2016. Tugann an earnáil treasach pictiúr difreáilte: treocht dhearfach i seirbhísí pearsanta (m.sh. seirbhísí leighis agus altranais), treocht diúltach go soiléir i seirbhísí a bhaineann le cuideachta (e.g. seirbhísí airgeadais agus dlí, faisnéis agus seirbhísí a bhaineann le cumarsáid) agus níos lú treochta diúltacha ar sheirbhísí iompair, trádála, cóiríochta agus lónadóireachta.<br/><br/>Margadh an tsaothair:<br/><br/>Rialaítear an chuid is mó de na gairmeacha sa Ghearmáin agus ní féidir rochtain a fháil orthu ach amháin leis an gcáilíocht ábhartha.<br/><br/>Dáiltear an dífhostaíocht go míchothrom idir iad siúd a bhfuil cáilíochtaí íseal-leibhéal acu.<br/><br/>Tá méadú tagtha ar an mbearna le linn na géarchéime mar go bhfuil oibrithe neamhoilte níos leochailí don dífhostaíocht. Sa bhliain 2018, ní raibh an ráta dífhostaíochta de dhaoine a bhfuil oideachas meánscoile agus iar-mheánscoile acu ach beagán os cionn ráta dífhostaíochta daoine a bhfuil oideachas treasach acu (2.9% i gcomparáid le 1.9%). Mar sin féin, bhí riosca i bhfad níos airde dífhostaíochta ag daoine íseal-oilte (níos lú ná an mheánscoil) agus an ráta ag 8.5 %.<br/><br/>Tháinig ardú ar ráta fostaíochta 20 go 34 céim de chuid GG bliain d’aois ó 87.6% in 2014 go 89.7% i 2018[11] tábla Eurostat edat_fse_24 [eastós 16.5.2019].<br/><br/>Bhí an méadú (+2.1pp) ar fhostaíocht céimithe 20-34 bliana d’aois VET i 2014-18 níos airde ná an méadú ar fhostaíocht de gach céimithe 20-34 bliain d’aois (+1.5 pp) sa tréimhse chéanna sa Ghearmáin (12[12]NB:Banna in amshraith. Tábla Eurostat data_fse_24 [eastós 16.5.2019]).<br/><br/>Tá an-tóir ar 57.4% sa Ghearmáin ar an gcuid is mó de na tiománaithe seachtracha a bhfuil tionchar acu ar fhorbairtí VET sa Ghearmáin, i gcomparáid le mórchuid na mBallstát eile, ar an oideachas tríú leibhéal in ICSE-4. Is féidir é seo a nascadh leis an bhfíric freisin, is bealach tarraingteach é an phrintíseacht agus fiú roghnaíonn céimithe tánaisteacha uachtaracha.<br/><br/>Daonra (25 go 64 bliana d’aois) de réir an leibhéil is airde oideachais a baineadh amach in 2018<br/><br/>Chun tuilleadh eolais a fháil faoi VET san ardoideachas sa Ghearmáin. Páipéar taighde Cedefop; Uimh 70.<br/><br/>Leanann mná agus fir óga orthu féin a bheith an-difriúil ar mhargadh VET sa Ghearmáin.Baineann sé seo ní amháin leis na cosáin oiliúna a ghlacann cailíní agus buachaillí, ach freisin leis na gairmeacha oiliúna a roghnaíonn siad. Mar shampla, tagraítear d’aos óg na bhfear sa chóras dé-GG (os cionn 60%), agus d’óg na mban in oiliúint lán-aimseartha scoile (75%), i ngairmeacha cúraim sláinte, oideachais agus sóisialta den chuid is mó.<br/><br/>Sna cláir printíseachta, is iad na cúig gairmeacha is fearr d’fhir teicneoir meicitreonaice ngluaisteán, teicneoir leictreonaice, speisialtóir TF, gléasra agus meicnic thionsclaíocha. I measc na bpríntís baineann, is iad na cúig shlí bheatha is fearr ná cúntóir bainistíochta oifige, cúntóir leighis, altra fiaclóireachta, saleswoman miondíola agus saleswoman.<br/><br/>Luathbhéile ó oideachas agus oiliúint:<br/><br/>Tá laghdú 11% ar sciar na luathfhágálaithe ón oideachas agus ón oiliúint in 2009 go dtí 10.3% i 2018 agus tá beagnach an sprioc náisiúnta bainte amach acu don bhliain 2020 nach mó ná 10%.<br/><br/>Cuirtear tacaíocht ar leith ar fáil a dhíríonn ar dhaoine óga a dteastaíonn cúnamh uathu chun gairmoiliúint a chur i gcrích. Is ranganna speisialta iad an rollú agus bíonn meantóireacht shocheacnamaíocha in éineacht le cúrsaí sóisialta chun cuidiú le printísigh easnaimh teanga agus oideachais a shárú agus eolas speisialaithe a fháil i rith trí huaire sa tseachtain ar a laghad. Tháinig an dlí lena mbunaítear an beart sin i bhfeidhm i mí na Bealtaine 2015. In 2017, ba thairbhithe (13.2017: EUR 97.1 milliún) an t-earrach: BMBF (2018). Berfbidungsbericht 2018 [Tuarascáil ar gairmoideachas agus oiliúint 2018] Bonn: BMBF, lch. 121. Léirigh sé seo sciar de 2.7% de na printíseachtaí go léir in 2017. Cabhraíonn sé le printísigh éirí as an oiliúint, caidrimh oiliúna a chothú agus oiliúint ghairmiúil iomlán a chur ar fáil. Is féidir le daoine a bhfuil deacrachtaí acu oiliúint bhreise a fháil ó oibrithe deonacha sinsearacha atá ag obair chun cosc a chur ar thionscnamh maidir le titim amach oiliúna, VA. Is gairmithe ar scor iad na saineolaithe sinsearacha a bhfuil taithí leathan acu ina réimse oibre faoi seach.[14]Hismann, A. (2018). Treoir agus for-rochtain do dhaoine neamhghníomhacha agus dífhostaithe – an Ghearmáin. p_ReferNet.pdf)<br/><br/>Tá bearta sonracha ag díriú ar dhaoine óga a dteastaíonn tacaíocht uathu níos luaithe, i.e. teastas ginearálta fágála scoile a fháil agus an t-aistriú ón scoil a dhéanamh chuig oiliúint: áirítear oiliúint ghairme, oiliúint tosaigh, agus oiliúint ullmhúcháin VET ann. Tá na bearta seo ar fad mar chuid den chlár slabhraí Oideachais, a bhfuil cur chuige láidir coisctheach ([15]BMBF (2018). Berfiscbuldungsbericht 2018 [Tuarascáil ar gairmoideachas agus oiliúint 2018] Bonn: BMBF, lch. 90.<br/><br/>Rannpháirtíocht i bhfoghlaim ar feadh an tsaoil:<br/><br/>Tugann foghlaim ar feadh an tsaoil deiseanna oiliúna d’aosaigh, lena n-áirítear luathfhágálaithe ón oideachas.<br/><br/>Mhéadaigh rannpháirtíocht i bhfoghlaim ar feadh an tsaoil sa Ghearmáin beagán ó 2014 go 2018 ó 8.0% go 8.2%, ach bhí sé fós faoi bhun meán AE-28 (1.8% agus 11.1% in 2014 agus 2018, faoi seach).<br/><br/>Áirítear leis an dtagarmharc Eorpach foghlaim neamhfhoirmeálta agus fhoirmiúil sna ceithre seachtaine deireanacha roimh an suirbhé (suirbhé ar fhórsa saothair) i measc freagróirí idir 25 agus 64 bliana d’aois. Sa suirbhé oideachais aosaigh, cuirtear ceist ar fhreagróirí faoi ghníomhaíochtaí foghlama le 12 mhí anuas. Sa chás seo, tá an ráta rannpháirtíochta san fhoghlaim ar feadh an tsaoil sa Ghearmáin i bhfad níos airde: 52% (i gcomparáid le meán 45.1% in AE-28).<br/><br/>Tosaíonn oideachas lánaimseartha éigeantach ag sé bliana d’aois agus maireann sé naoi mbliana (nó 10 mbliana ag brath ar an Stát Chónaidhme). Ina dhiaidh sin, is féidir le daoine óga a roghnaigh gan clár oideachais lánaimseartha a leanúint freastal ar scoil (gairmiúil) ar feadh trí bliana mar chuid dá gcuid oiliúna sa chuideachta.<br/><br/>I ndiaidh ceithre bliana den bhunscoil do gach duine, roinntear na cosáin oideachais i gcóras na fo-roinnte, ina bhfuil cláir thánaisteacha níos ísle (go dtí grád 9 nó 10) agus i gcláir thánaisteacha (go dtí grád 12 nó 13).<br/><br/>Tá an Ghearmáin ar cheann de na tíortha Eorpacha ina bhfuil foghlaim ar an bpost ina gcuid traidisiúnta den chóras oideachais: is é an clár printíseachta (déchóras, le dhá ionad foghlama: 70% den obair bunaithe ar scoil agus 30%) an príomhcholún de VET. Baineann gairm-aistear le stádas oideachais amháin de dhá chéim bhunscoile, agus is féidir dul chun cinn a dhéanamh trí chláir éagsúla rialaithe VET ag leibhéal an iar-mheánscoile agus ag leibhéal na treaslainne níos mó.<br/><br/>Tá oideachas tosaigh agus leanúnach i gcóras GG na Gearmáine; i dteannta ghníomhaíocht scoilbhunaithe, tá ról mór ag an obair (BLB) i bhformhór na gclár a chuirtear ar fáil ag leibhéil thánaisteacha agus threasacha. Tá na roghanna foghlama VET seo a leanas ann, lena n-áirítear laindéal na nithe seo a leanas:<br/><br/>Is é an clár printíseachta ar leibhéal meánoideachais uachtarach (leibhéal EQF 4) an príomhcholún sa VET agus meallann sé céimí meánscolaíochta uachtair freisin. Is cláir chuimsitheacha VET iad comhthreomhar leis na printíseachtaí ag an leibhéal uasta tánaisteach (leibhéal 2 go 4), atá difriúil ó thaobh rochtana, faid, cineálacha agus leibhéil cháilíochta a dtagann siad orthu. Spléachadh ar an ngairmoideachas agus ar an ngairmoiliúint sa Ghearmáin. Lucsamburg: Oifig na bhFoilseachán.<br/><br/>Is é an uirlis is tábhachtaí chun measúnú a dhéanamh ar thorthaí foghlama neamhfhoirmeálta a chur isteach sna scrúduithe deiridh ar a dtugtar an Exten-Prüfung (scrúdú ar iarrthóirí seachtracha, i.e., na cinn nach bhfuil bainteach le clár foirmiúil gairmoiliúna) [18] Faoi Alt 45 (2) den Acht um Oiliúint Gairmbhála (BisiG). Faoin bhforáil seo, is féidir daoine a ligean isteach i scrúdú deiridh ar ghairm bheatha aitheanta a bhfuil oiliúint fhoirmiúil (cumar slí bheatha oiliúna aitheanta) más rud é go gcuireann siad fianaise ar fáil gur fostaíodh iad sa tslí bheatha ábhartha ar feadh tréimhse nach lú ná leathuaire ar a laghad fad a bheidh siad forordaithe don tréimhse oiliúna tosaigh.<br/><br/>Ar leibhéal na treasóige, tá trí chéim sa ghairmcháilíochtaí ar leith agus sna scrúduithe a fuarthas ón nGearmáin. Tá difríocht idir iad agus riachtanais inniúlachta agus an imscaradh oibríochta gaolmhar i gcuideachtaí. Éilíonn iontráil ar leibhéal 7 cáilíochtaí cáilíochtaí leibhéal 6; ní gá cáilíocht leibhéal 5 a bhaint amach ach is féidir í a fháil go díreach tar éis VET sa chóras dé déach agus is gá taithí oibre a bheith agat den chuid is mó (tá gá le sárcheardas, teicneoir nó saincháilíochtaí).<br/><br/>Murab ionann agus na rialacháin oiliúna le haghaidh IVET sa chóras déach, ní chuimsíonn na rialacháin oiliúna ardteicneolaíochta seo curaclam a dhéantar a rialú go haonair; déanann siad scrúduithe a shainiú agus a thuairisciú. Ar na gnéithe eile nach mór a shonrú sna rialacháin ardoiliúna, áirítear (§ 53 para. 2 BioG, § 42 par. 2 HOO):<br/><br/>(a) ainmniú na hardcháilíochtaí;<br/><br/>(b) aidhm, ábhar agus ceanglais an scrúdaithe;<br/><br/>(c) ceanglais maidir le daoine a ligean isteach;<br/><br/>(d) nós imeachta scrúdúcháin.<br/><br/>De ghnáth, bíonn cúrsa lán oiliúna gairme agus/nó taithí ghairmiúil chuí ag teastáil chun dul isteach i scrúdú. Tá na rialacháin seo leagtha síos ag an BMBF trí chomhaontú leis na haireachtaí inniúla agus tar éis dul i gcomhairle le bord príomhúil (Hupatuschuss) an BBB. Tugann ardoiliúint ghairme mar mháistircheard-cheardbhall (Feachtas) teideal don sealbhóir trádáil cheirde a chleachtadh go neamhspleách, chun fostaithe a dhéanamh agus chun oiliúint a chur ar an sealbhóir, agus chun rochtain a fháil ar chúrsaí i gceardaithe ag ollscoileanna eolaíochtaí feidhmeacha (UASanna,<br/><br/>Foclóir) chomh maith le hollscoileanna.<br/><br/>Ní thaifeadtar sonraí faoin gclár seo go hiomlán i staitisticí ICSE-97 ar dhá chúis. Ar dtús, ní gá ardchlár gairme leis na scrúduithe (ISCED 655; EQF 6) a thairiscint ag scoileanna trádála agus teicniúla, a rialaítear de réir dhlí an Stáit. Bíonn riachtanais iontrála éagsúla de réir ábhair: de ghnáth bíonn cáilíocht ag teastáil ó iarratasóir i ngairm aitheanta oiliúna atá oiriúnach don ábhar roghnaithe, agus bíonn taithí oibre ábhartha bliain amháin ar a laghad, nó cáilíocht ó scoil ghairmiúil lánaimseartha agus ó thaithí oibre ábhartha cúig bliana ar a laghad aige. Is féidir ardchláracha a leanúint mar chláir lánaimseartha nó páirtaimseartha (ar deireadh idir bliain agus trí bliana) agus bíonn cáilíocht ghairme Stáit mar thoradh orthu (e.g. oideachasóir; theicneoir). Glacann an scoláire feidhmeanna leitheadacha freagrachta agus bainistíochta san ionad oibre. Cuireann roinnt scoileanna trádála agus teicniúla cláir ar fáil freisin a mbíonn cáilíocht iontrála fhoirmiúil acu d’ollscoileanna na n-eolaíochtaí feidhmeacha. Tá siad ann do na réimsí ceirde seo a leanas: talmhaíocht, dearadh, teicneolaíocht, gnó agus cúram sóisialta. Críochann siad le scrúdú deiridh Stáit faoi dhlí an Stáit.<br/><br/>Cuireann déchláir (leibhéil 6 agus 7) dhá ionad foghlama (an t-ionad oibre agus an institiúid oideachais) ar fáil agus cuireann ollscoileanna eolaíochtaí feidhmeacha (UASanna, Fachochschulen), ollscoil débhrá (D Dual Hochschulen), ollscoileanna an oideachais chomh maith le roinnt ollscoileanna. Is cláir staidéir déthaobhúla iad timpeall ceathrú clár na Stát Aontaithe ([19]) bunaithe ar: Hippach-Schneider, U; Huismann, A.2019. Gairmoideachas agus oiliúint san Eoraip: An Ghearmáin. Cedefop FREE VET i dtuarascálacha 2018.<br/><br/>Tá dé- VET, a úsáidtear mar shionainm le haghaidh printíseachtaí sa Ghearmáin, fós an-tarraingteach. Go háirithe mar gheall ar an gcaoi a nascann sé foghlaim agus obair, chomh maith le scoileanna agus cuideachtaí, is cosúil gur samhail rathúil é an córas chun an t-aistriú ón scoil a struchtúrú ó shaol oibre. Le haghaidh an tasc seo, cuireann an Stát dianobair oiliúna i gcrích faoi láthair. Is í an Stát a údaróidh na seomraí agus tá siad ag gníomhú go hoifigiúil mar institiúid phoiblí. Nuair a dhéantar an scrúdú deiridh a rith, faigheann na printísigh teastas seomra ranga chun an oiliúint sin a chur i gcrích, agus aithnítear an deimhniú cáilíochta seo go hiomlán agus go bhfuil an-mhuiníneach uirthi i measc fostóirí.<br/><br/>Maireann printíseacht sa chóras débhliantúla de ghnáth trí bliana ([21] Níl ach dhá bhliain ag teastáil i roinnt gairmeacha agus tá rialacháin ann freisin a ligeann tréimhse oiliúna níos giorra do phrintíseachtaí le hAbtur (an teastas fágála scoile a cheadaíonn dul isteach san ardoideachas). Ar an meán, tógann daoine óga VET ag aois 19.7 (9 [22]BBB (2018). Téann an clár oideachais agus oiliúna gairmiúla gairmiúla leanúnaí leanúnaí de chuid Berfbustingsbericht 2018 i bhfeidhm. Ní mór oideachas éigeantach a bheith curtha i gcrích sula dtosaíonn tú ar VET.Níl aon riachtanais rochtana foirmiúla eile ann ach roghnaíonn cuideachtaí a gcuid cprintíseach agus an chuid is mó díobh23]BBB (2018). Dátareport zum Berfbidungsbericht 2018 [Tuairiscigh sonraí na tuarascála gairmoideachais agus gairmoiliúna 2018] Bonn: BBB, lch. 132. Lean an grúpa seo an dá chonair oideachais ag leibhéal meán-iarchéime i ndiaidh na céime, agus an cháilíocht ghairmiúil ina dhiaidh sin. In ainneoin gur ‘iarbhunoideachas’ atá á aicmiú mar ‘iarbhunoideachas’, is céimí ardleibhéil a measann céimithe ar dtús gur rogha mhalartach iad san oideachas treasach.<br/><br/>Freastalaíonn na printísigh ar scoil ghairme ar feadh lá nó dhó sa tseachtain, áit a múintear eolas teoiriciúil agus praiticiúil den chuid is mó dóibh agus a bhaineann lena ngairm féin; glacann siad ranganna ar ábhair ghinearálta amhail cúrsaí eacnamaíochta, staidéir shóisialta agus teangacha iasachta. Tarraingítear curaclam creatlaí do gach slí bheatha aitheanta oiliúna de réir na rialachán oiliúna.Is é príomhaidhm na hoiliúna ná cur ar chumas daoine óga cumas cuimsitheach gairmiúil a fháil. Tar éis dóibh an phrintíseacht a chríochnú, ba cheart go mbeidís in ann a ndualgais a chomhlíonadh mar fhostaithe go héifeachtúil, go nuálach, go neamhspleách agus i gcomhar le daoine eile. Ní mór an raon inniúlachtaí a léiriú i scrúduithe a rialaítear leis an dlí (An tAcht Oiliúna Gairmoideachais, BioG). Tá na scrúduithe deiridh dírithe ar chleachtadh gairme, i.e., ar riachtanais oibre agus ar phróisis na gairme. Déantar meastóireacht ar fheidhmíocht in ábhair ghinearálta trí thuarascálacha scoile.<br/><br/>Cuirtear áiteanna do phrintísigh ar fáil i bhfiontair agus in institiúidí poiblí araon.I gcás ina iompróidh siad na costais na hoiliúna laistigh de chuideachta agus íoc as an luach saothair oiliúna. Rialaítear é seo le comhaontú comhchoiteann agus méadaíonn sé gach bliain oiliúna, ag meánmhéid maidir le tríú cuid den phá tosaigh d’oibrí oilte. Sonraítear na hinniúlachtaí gairmiúla atá le fáil trí oiliúint in-seirbhíse i rialacháin oiliúna agus áirítear iad ag an bhfiontar oiliúna i bplean oiliúna aonair. Ráthaíonn ceanglais cheangailteach na rialachán oiliúna caighdeán náisiúnta aonfhoirmeach. Ó 2016 i leith, áfach, tá FBManna ag cur chun cinn sna hionaid oiliúna sin trí cheannach trealaimh dhigiteach chomh maith le tionscadail phíolótaí roghnaithe chun próisis teagaisc agus foghlama a oiriúnú ([24 cinn níos mó Ba é an t-ullmhúchán do na printísigh de réir na hearnála tráchtála fostaíochta mar a leanas in 2016: 58.7% in earnáil na trádála agus an tionscail, 2.7% i ngairmeacha beatha, 2.8% san earnáil phoiblí, i dtalmhaíocht agus 0.4% i bpiantacht. Tá titim i gconarthaí nua printíseachta ó 2008 i leith, bliain na géarchéime airgeadais (ach eisceacht amháin, in 2011, nuair a tugadh conarthaí printíseachta nua chun críche). Síníodh an treocht anuas seo idir 2016 agus 2017: 0.6% níos mó conarthaí printíseachta in 2017 ná sa bhliain roimhe sin.<br/><br/>Tá an margadh printíseachta fós á thréithriú ag méadú ar fhadhbanna meaitseála.Tá sé ag éirí níos deacra gach bliain soláthar oiliúna cuideachtaí a mheaitseáil (2017: 57226) le héileamh daoine óga ar phoist oiliúna (2017: 603 510). Tá sé seo soiléir go háirithe ón bhfíric go bhfuil poist fholmha (2017: 48 937, 12.6% níos mó ná 2016 agus luach is airde ó 1995) mar chion forála méadaithe arís, ó 7.7% go 8.6%. Mar sin féin, tá an sciar d’iarratasóirí nár éirigh leo mar chion den éileamh a aithníodh go hoifigiúil do 2017 fós sách ard ach cobhsaí, ag 13.3% Bhí tionchar ar leith ag ganntanas iarratasóirí ar earnáil na ceirdeanna oilte agus ar thrádáil. Tá sé mar aidhm ag go leor beart beartais phoiblí dul i ngleic leis na forbairtí seo.<br/><br/>Cineálacha cáilíochta fágála scoile a fhaightear difriúil i measc na bpríntís a bhfuil conarthaí oiliúna nua curtha i gcrích acu. Mar a bhí sna blianta beaga anuas, ba é an grúpa ba mhó in 2016 iad siúd a raibh an teastas fágála meánscoile idirmheánach (mutter Schulschlus), ag 42.8% (215 976). Bhí cáilíocht iontrála níos airde (Abitur) ag beagnach 30% (144 630) díobh siúd a tugadh i gcrích, i seilbh cáilíocht iontrála ardoideachais (Abitur). Bhí deimhniú fágála dara leibhéal níos ísle ag thart ar aon cheann acu (Huptschulabsus). Bhí cion na n-oiliúnaithe nua gan deimhniú fágála scoile an-íseal ag 3.1% (15 876) ([25]BBB (2018).<br/><br/>Is minic a bhíonn sé deacair agus fada go n-aistreofaí daoine óga a bhfuil cúlra imirce acu, aistriú ón oideachas ginearálta go VET. Léiríonn an suirbhé deiridh (2016) BA/BB i measc iar-iarratasóirí dé-cháilíochta go raibh socrúchán faighte ag duine óg a bhfuil cúlra imirce acu agus go raibh an t-iarratasóir cláraithe leis an ngníomhaireacht fostaíochta cónaidhme (BA) agus go raibh sé tosaithe acu ar phrintíseacht cheannasach. I gcodarsnacht leis sin, bhí 42% de na daoine sin nár chuir cúlra imirce tús le printíseacht den sórt sin ([26]BBB (2018). An Tuarascáil Bhliantúil 2011 ar an Tuarascáil ar Oideachas agus ar Oiliúint i gcomhair na gairme 2018]. Bonn: BBB, lch. 326.<br/><br/>Tháinig méadú suntasach ar líon na ndídeanaithe a chuireann isteach ar thearmann, den chuid is mó ó 2015 i leith agus a chuireann isteach ar shocrúchán printíseachta (le clárú ag gníomhaireacht fostaíochta) ón 10 Meán Fómhair 2016 go dtí 26 428 i Meán Fómhair 2017. Bhí sé beagnach 5% de na hiarrthóirí GG dé-Ghaeilge cláraithe.<br/><br/>Cáilíochtaí breise<br/><br/>Ó leasaíodh an tAcht Oiliúna Gairm-Oideachais i 2005 (27) is féidir ‘cáilíochtaí breise códaithe’ a sholáthar i gcomhthéacs printíseachta. Áirítear leis sin ‘scileanna, eolas agus cáilíochtaí breise’ (...) chun inniúlachtaí gairme a fhorlíonadh nó a leathnú’ (Treoir 2005 (2), atá ar ancaire sna rialacháin oiliúna agus chun dul níos faide ná an phróifíl slí bheatha oiliúna. Forlíonann na cáilíochtaí breise seo na rialacháin oiliúna. Chomh maith leis sin, atá nasctha le rialachán oiliúna, tá go leor cáilíochtaí breise ann. Maidir leis na hinnealtóirí meicitreonaice amháin, tá beagnach 400 cáilíocht bhreise roghnach ann ([28]Féach bunachar sonraí AusbidungPlus: agus Berfidungssetz 2005:<br/><br/>Mar sin féin, níl na cáilíochtaí breise seo dírithe go leor ar phróifíl cháilíochta a leathnú mar chuid den phróifíl ghairme sin, ach i gcás breisithe nó speisialtóirí a bhaineann le hábhar. Sa chás seo, tá siad difriúil ó na cáilíochtaí breise códaithe, a fheidhmíonn go sainráite le síneadh na próifíle gairme oiliúna. Tá ceann de na cáilíochtaí breise neamhchódaithe seo i gcáilíochtaí idirnáisiúnta; áirítear leo sin cúrsaí teanga iasachta agus bainistíocht idirnáisiúnta. Faigheann thart ar aon trian de na printísigh i gcáilíochtaí breise traenáil sa réimse sin.<br/><br/>Ceadaíonn cáilíochtaí breise múnlú solúbtha oiliúna sa chuideachta maidir leis na ceanglais cháilíochta sa chuideachta. Cuireann sé sin ar chumas cuideachtaí freagairt go pras ar riachtanais scileanna atá ag athrú, rud atá ag éirí níos tábhachtaí mar gheall ar fhorbairtí sa digitiú. Ag an am céanna, is deis tarraingteach é do dhaoine óga a gcáilíochtaí gairme a uasghrádú. Tá difríochtaí móra idir cáilíochtaí breise atá liostaithe i mbunachar sonraí AusbidungsPlus ([29] ar feadh tréimhse: tá sé idir 40 agus 1 000 uair an chloig chun cáilíocht bhreise a fháil. Cuireann comhlachtaí oiliúna agus gairmscoileanna cáilíochtaí breise ar fáil go príomha.I measc na bpríomhsholáthraithe cáilíochtaí breise atá ag cumainn tráchtála agus tionscail chomh maith le seomraí na n-eardaíochta agus a n-ionad oiliúna.<br/><br/>Tá VET bunaithe ar ghairmeacha aitheanta náisiúnta agus ar rialacháin ghairmoiliúna, a ráthaíonn caighdeán náisiúnta.Tá an rialtas cónaidhme freagrach as an déábhar oiliúna córais a dhearadh do na gairmeacha atá aitheanta aige. Cinntíonn aitheantas náisiúnta ceangailteach ó thaobh na ngairmeacha oiliúna go bhfuil na bunphrionsabail a comhaontaíodh le tionscal agus go gcuirtear na Stáit san áireamh agus go gcloíonn an oiliúint maidir le slí bheatha aitheanta leis na rialacháin a ghlac an rialtas cónaidhme. Níl freagrachtaí an rialtais cónaidhme teoranta do chomhaontuithe comhpháirteacha a chur chun feidhme; glacann sé freisin bearta neamhspleácha chun oiliúint dhá-ar-chéim a chur chun cinn. Áirítear leis na bearta sin cláir bhuan thacaíochta mar aon le cláir chistiúcháin speisialta, a bhfuil sé mar aidhm leo, mar shampla, poist bhreise oiliúna a chruthú i réigiúin nach bhfuil chomh coitianta céanna. Tá an Rialtas Cónaidhme freagrach as tionscadail taighde speisialta a chinntiú go ndéantar an VET a nuashonrú i gcónaí.Is í an Aireacht Cónaidhme Oideachais agus Taighde (33]Bundesimitrium für Buildingung und Forschung (BMBF). Áirítear orthu sin an tAcht Oiliúna Gairm-Treoraithe ([34]Beruffsbidungsez (BBiG), an tuarascáil bhliantúil VET, cur chun feidhme na gclár chun feabhas a chur ar an maoirseacht agus maoiniú dlí a dhéantar ar an Institiúid Chónaidhme um VET ([35]Bundes Institute für Berfbidung (BBB).<br/><br/>Ar bhonn náisiúnta, is í an Institiúid Chónaidhme um GGG an institiúid lárnach d’fhoirgneamh comhdhearcadh idir na páirtithe uile atá bainteach le VET.Déanann sé taighde ar oiliúint in-chomhlacht agus soláthraíonn sé seirbhísí agus comhairle do na soláthróirí rialtais cónaidhme agus VET. Cuireann a phríomhbhord ceithre pháirtí comhairle ar an rialtas maidir le saincheisteanna bunúsacha oiliúna ghairmeacha in-chuideachta agus tá baint aige le caighdeáin a leagan síos agus rialacháin oiliúna a dhearadh.<br/><br/>Is é cúram na n-eisiúcháin cónaidhme atá freagrach as gach réimse ceirde aitheantas a thabhairt do ghairmeacha aonair a éilíonn oiliúint fhoirmiúil. I bhformhór na gcásanna, is é seo an Aireacht Cónaidhme Gnóthaí Eacnamaíocha agus Fuinnimh ([36]Bundesmintium für Wirtschaft und Energye (BMWi). Tá gá i gcónaí le formheas a fháil ón aireacht oideachais, agus mar sin cuireann an Aireacht comhordú agus treoir ar fáil le haghaidh beartas VET do gach slí bheatha oiliúna.<br/><br/>Ról an rialtais Stáit<br/><br/>De réir na gConarthaí, is ar an Stát a bhíonn an fhreagracht as oideachas scoile a aireachtaí oideachais agus cultúrtha ([37] Landisteren für Buildingung, Wisconsinchaft und Kultur.). Glacann a n-airí páirt i buanchoiste ([38]Kultusminerkonferz (KKK) chun a chinntiú go mbeidh leibhéal áirithe aonfhoirmeachta agus inchomparáideacht ann, go háirithe i mbeartais scoile agus ardoideachais. Is moltaí amháin iad na cinntí buana ón gcoiste, agus ní bhíonn siad ach ina gceangal dlí ar an Stát aonair. Tá coistí gairm-oiliúna sna Stáit, le hionadaíocht comhionann ar fhostóirí, ar fhostaithe agus ar na húdaráis Stáit is airde.
